## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[write_process_route_upload] --> B[Create ProcessRouteUpload]
    B --> C[Set default values]
    C --> D[Set group_id, solution_id, identifier]
    D --> E{shipper_or_carrier?}
    E -->|SHIPPER| F[Set identifier_key to shipper_location_code]
    E -->|CARRIER| G[Set identifier_key to carrier_location_code]
    F --> H[Write to data store]
    G --> H
    H --> I[Return result]
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[check_location] --> B[Invoke get_location_by_code]
    B --> C{Location exists?}
    C -->|Yes| D[Return success: True, comment: Resolved location is created]
    C -->|No| E[Invoke get_unlinked_location_by_code]
    E --> F{Unresolved location exists?}
    F -->|Yes| G[Return success: False, comment: Unresolved location is created]
    F -->|No| H[Return success: False, comment: Location is not valid]
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Client
    participant TripLegLocationBusinessLogic
    participant ProcessRouteUploadPostgresqlMapping
    participant ProcessRouteUpload
    Client->>TripLegLocationBusinessLogic: write_process_route_upload(request_id, solution_id, location_code, shipper_or_carrier)
    TripLegLocationBusinessLogic->>ProcessRouteUpload: create instance
    TripLegLocationBusinessLogic->>ProcessRouteUpload: set default values
    TripLegLocationBusinessLogic->>ProcessRouteUpload: set group_id, solution_id, identifier
    alt shipper_or_carrier == SHIPPER
        TripLegLocationBusinessLogic->>ProcessRouteUpload: set identifier_key to shipper_location_code
    else shipper_or_carrier == CARRIER
        TripLegLocationBusinessLogic->>ProcessRouteUpload: set identifier_key to carrier_location_code
    end
    TripLegLocationBusinessLogic->>ProcessRouteUploadPostgresqlMapping: write(process_route_upload)
    ProcessRouteUploadPostgresqlMapping-->>TripLegLocationBusinessLogic: result
    TripLegLocationBusinessLogic-->>Client: return result
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Client
    participant TripLegLocationBusinessLogic
    participant InvokeLocation
    Client->>TripLegLocationBusinessLogic: check_location(organization_id, location_code)
    TripLegLocationBusinessLogic->>InvokeLocation: invoke_get_location_by_code(organization_id, location_code)
    InvokeLocation-->>TripLegLocationBusinessLogic: location
    alt location exists
        TripLegLocationBusinessLogic-->>Client: {success: True, comment: Resolved location is created}
    else location is None
        TripLegLocationBusinessLogic->>InvokeLocation: invoke_get_unlinked_location_by_code(organization_id, location_code)
        InvokeLocation-->>TripLegLocationBusinessLogic: unresolved_location
        alt unresolved_location exists
            TripLegLocationBusinessLogic-->>Client: {success: False, comment: Unresolved location is created}
        else unresolved_location is None
            TripLegLocationBusinessLogic-->>Client: {success: False, comment: Location is not valid}
        end
    end
```
